    1566: Champions League Betting
    1568: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    1615: Accumulators
    1617: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    1895: Champions League Betting
    1897: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.

    1940: Doubles & Trebles
    1942: Fancy two or three teams to win? You can bet on both or all three happening for the chance to get even bigger odds by creating a double or treble.
    1944: Accumulators
    1946: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

1962: SW stands for "score and win". Betting on an SW market means you're simply betting on the match result and that both teams will score in the game. Or, you could choose a player to score and a team to win as part of a wincast.

    2272: Doubles & Trebles
    2274: Fancy two or three teams to win? You can bet on both or all three happening for the chance to get even bigger odds by creating a double or treble.
    2276: Accumulators
    2278: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

2294: SW stands for "score and win". Betting on an SW market means you're simply betting on the match result and that both teams will score in the game. Or, you could choose a player to score and a team to win as part of a wincast.

    2299: Keep it fun: bet responsibly - as soon as it stops being fun, think about taking a step back.

    2303: Know your limits: set a budget - this will help you stay in control of what you spend, and keep betting fun.

    2615: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them.     2664: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    3049: Accumulators, or "accas", follow the same format as doubles and trebles: all bet selections must win for the bet to come in. The difference is that with an acca, you can add four or more selections to your bet slip, with increasing odds for the more picks in your acca.

    3329: Champions League Betting
    3331: The Champions League is Europe’s premier club competition, bringing together the continent’s biggest teams in an expanded league-format tournament. After the qualifying rounds, 36 clubs enter the league phase, where each team plays eight opponents. The top-ranked sides progress directly to the Round of 16, while teams placed in the mid-table positions compete in play-offs to join them. From there, the tournament continues with traditional two-legged knockout rounds, delivering months of high-quality, high-stakes, high-drama football.
    3333: At William Hill, we have pre-tournament odds under the Champions League betting, plus a host of other odds throughout the tournament, from group winners to top goalscorers.
